        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3156638460" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11394427109794584632">As someone who loves the legend of Atlantis, I really enjoyed this book. At the macrocosmic level, the book contains tensions between free will and destiny as well as love and duty. These tensions cause conflict between characters and within them, making for a dramatic story and a fast pace. I also loved the various elements of magic infusing every part of this book. There are Watchers, Nephilim, etc., and each group of entities has its own values and agendas. In terms of setting, I very much ap</span>
  <span id="freeText11394427109794584632" style="display:none">As someone who loves the legend of Atlantis, I really enjoyed this book. At the macrocosmic level, the book contains tensions between free will and destiny as well as love and duty. These tensions cause conflict between characters and within them, making for a dramatic story and a fast pace. I also loved the various elements of magic infusing every part of this book. There are Watchers, Nephilim, etc., and each group of entities has its own values and agendas. In terms of setting, I very much appreciated how some of the characters' names reflect Classical Antiquity. I personally believe Atlantis was a reference to Minoan civilization, so some of the Greek-ish and Roman-ish sounding names was a nice touch. That said, the allusions to Classical cultures is not a necessity for a book on Atlantis :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="11394427109794584632" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('OTvmAlZtJ41bDiTxWUat+xzanTXL/foiDDy7nGSIYriGSR1LSfKdHXfbJpWWWnmBmIW0J6cqm8U6OhNe5zZ6BA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('i8GxYqYaAlsWoNznwXyrh/n0Ph4EVItNKwVnITslcyc0s0oruYW4yzp13oMOYH/9fasXDGiD6qodA8/juJtrmw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer11324499695082584227">I have always been fascinated with Atlantis. I discovered it when I was sixteen during a phase where I was dissatisfied with my religion. I spent a lot of time in the library, studying books on various world religions. The study of Hinduism led me to past lives, and then to the new age section where I found the work of Edgar Cayce. He was known as the sleeping prophet, and was famous for his past </span>
  <span id="freeText11324499695082584227" style="display:none">I have always been fascinated with Atlantis. I discovered it when I was sixteen during a phase where I was dissatisfied with my religion. I spent a lot of time in the library, studying books on various world religions. The study of Hinduism led me to past lives, and then to the new age section where I found the work of Edgar Cayce. He was known as the sleeping prophet, and was famous for his past life readings, particularly the ones in Atlantis. My imagination has been hooked since then. I have never been conventional. My whole life has been devoted to my artistic path. I have traveled for decades, embodying the famous quote from the Hobbit "Not all who wander are lost." <br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="11324499695082584227" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
